## üèóÔ∏è What the Prototype is Based On

### **Frontend MCP Server Foundation**

### **Progressive Conversational Interface Design**

‚Ä¢ **Post-ChatGPT Era UX**: Users now comfortable with conversational AI
‚Ä¢ **Automotive Context**: Diagnostics naturally involve questions and clarifications
‚Ä¢ **Hands-Free Operation**: Essential for drivers and mechanics working on vehicles
‚Ä¢ **Competitive Advantage**: Differentiates from traditional automotive apps

## üõ†Ô∏è Technical Architecture

### **Core Technology Stack**

### **Key Features Implemented**

## üì± Mobile-First Approach

## üöÄ Development Approach

This prototype serves as a design validation tool and development reference for the eventual React Native mobile apps. It's built to:

1. Validate UX Flows: Test complete user journeys before native development
2. Prove Technical Concepts: Demonstrate voice integration and conversational UI
3. Mobile Testing: Real device testing through mobile browsers
4. Stakeholder Demos: Interactive prototype for business validation

The prototype is essentially a high-fidelity interactive mockup that bridges the gap between static wireframes and the final React Native mobile 
applications, built using modern web technologies to simulate the mobile app experience.

‚úÖ Universal Design System - Works on iOS/Android/Web

‚Ä¢ **NativeBase**: Good but heavier, slower performance

## ‚úÖ Currently Working Features

### **1. ChatGPT-Style Interface**
‚Ä¢ **Clean chat layout** - Matches ChatGPT's design with Dixon Smart Repair branding
‚Ä¢ **Message bubbles** - User messages (blue, right-aligned) and AI messages (gray, left-aligned)
‚Ä¢ **Responsive design** - Works on web, iOS, and Android from single codebase

### **2. Basic Chat Functionality**
‚Ä¢ **Send messages** - Type in the input field and press "Send" or hit Enter
‚Ä¢ **AI responses** - Simulated AI responses with 2-second delay
‚Ä¢ **Typing indicator** - Shows "AI is typing..." during response generation
‚Ä¢ **Message history** - All messages persist during the session

### **3. Dixon Smart Repair Branding**
‚Ä¢ **Header branding** - "Dixon Smart Repair" title with "AI Automotive Diagnostics" subtitle
‚Ä¢ **Automotive colors** - Blue primary color (#1e40af) matching automotive theme
‚Ä¢ **Professional layout** - Clean, automotive-focused design

### **4. Mobile-Optimized Controls**
‚Ä¢ **Large touch targets** - 44px minimum for automotive use (gloved hands)
‚Ä¢ **+ Button** - Ready for photo/camera attachments (placeholder)
‚Ä¢ **Voice button** - üé§ microphone icon (placeholder)
‚Ä¢ **Hamburger menu** - Three-line menu button (placeholder)
‚Ä¢ **New Chat button** - Resets conversation to initial state

### **5. Cross-Platform Compatibility**
‚Ä¢ **Web browser** - Works in Chrome, Safari, Firefox
‚Ä¢ **iOS** - Can test via Expo Go app on iPhone
‚Ä¢ **Android** - Can test via Expo Go app on Android

## üß™ How to Test Current Features

### **Basic Chat Testing**
1. Type a message like "My car won't start" and press Send
2. Watch AI response - Should get automotive diagnostic response after 2 seconds
3. Try New Chat - Click "New Chat" button to reset conversation
4. Test input field - Try multiline messages, empty messages (Send disabled)

### **Mobile Testing** (if you have Expo Go app)
1. Scan QR code from terminal/browser
2. Test touch targets - All buttons should be easy to tap
3. Test responsive design - Rotate device, test different screen sizes

### **Visual Testing**
‚Ä¢ **Message alignment** - User messages right, AI messages left
‚Ä¢ **Color scheme** - Blue for user, gray for AI, automotive branding
‚Ä¢ **Typography** - Clear, readable text sizes
‚Ä¢ **Spacing** - Proper padding and margins

## üîÑ What's Next (Phase 2)

The next phase would add:
‚Ä¢ **Functional hamburger menu** with automotive sections
‚Ä¢ **Real voice input/output** 
‚Ä¢ **Photo/camera integration** for VIN scanning
‚Ä¢ **Conversation history** and persistence
‚Ä¢ **Automotive diagnostic flow** within chat

## üéØ Current Limitations

‚Ä¢ **Placeholder buttons** - Voice, camera, and menu buttons don't function yet

+      6: interface UseVoiceProps {
+      7:   onResult?: (transcript: string) => void
+      8:   onError?: (error: string) => void
+      9:   automotiveMode?: boolean
+     10: }
+     11: 
+     12: interface VoiceState {
+     13:   isListening: boolean
+     14:   isSupported: boolean
+     15:   isSpeaking: boolean
+     16:   isProcessing: boolean
+     17:   error: string | null
+     18: }
+     19: 
+     20: export function useVoice(props: UseVoiceProps = {}) {
+     21:   const { onResult, onError, automotiveMode = true } = props
+     22:   
+     23:   const [state, setState] = useState<VoiceState>({
+     24:     isListening: false,
+     25:     isSupported: true, // Assume supported for now
+     26:     isSpeaking: false,
+     27:     isProcessing: false,
+     28:     error: null,
+     29:   })
+     30: 
+     31:   const recordingRef = useRef<Audio.Recording | null>(null)
+     32:   const timeoutRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null)
+     33: 
+     34:   // Initialize audio permissions
+     35:   const initializeAudio = useCallback(async () => {
+     36:     try {
+     37:       const { status } = await Audio.requestPermissionsAsync()
+     38:       if (status !== 'granted') {
+     39:         throw new Error('Audio permission not granted')
+     40:       }
+     41:       
+     42:       await Audio.setAudioModeAsync({
+     43:         allowsRecordingIOS: true,
+     44:         playsInSilentModeIOS: true,
+     45:         shouldDuckAndroid: true,
+     46:         playThroughEarpieceAndroid: false,
+     47:         staysActiveInBackground: false,
+     48:       })
+     49:       
+     50:       return true
+     51:     } catch (error) {
+     52:       console.error('Audio initialization error:', error)
+     53:       onError?.('Failed to initialize audio permissions')
+     54:       return false
+     55:     }
+     56:   }, [onError])
+     57: 
+     58:   // Start voice recognition (mock implementation for prototype)
+     59:   const startListening = useCallback(async () => {
+     60:     if (state.isListening) return
+     61: 
+     62:     const audioInitialized = await initializeAudio()
+     63:     if (!audioInitialized) return
+     64: 
+     65:     setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isListening: true, error: null }))
+     66: 
+     67:     try {
+     68:       // Mock voice recognition for prototype
+     69:       // In production, this would use actual speech recognition
+     70:       
+     71:       // Simulate listening period
+     72:       timeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
+     73:         setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isListening: false, isProcessing: true }))
+     74:         
+     75:         // Simulate processing and return mock automotive phrases
+     76:         setTimeout(() => {
+     77:           const mockPhrases = [
+     78:             "My car won't start",
+     79:             "The brakes are squeaking",
+     80:             "Engine makes a rattling noise",
+     81:             "Check engine light is on",
+     82:             "Car pulls to the right when driving",
+     83:             "Air conditioning not working",
+     84:             "Battery seems dead",
+     85:             "Transmission is slipping"
+     86:           ]
+     87:           
+     88:           const randomPhrase = mockPhrases[Math.floor(Math.random() * mockPhrases.length)]
+     89:           onResult?.(randomPhrase)
+     90:           
+     91:           setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isProcessing: false }))
+     92:         }, 1500) // Processing time
+     93:         
+     94:       }, 3000) // Listening time
+     95:       
+     96:     } catch (error) {
+     97:       console.error('Voice recognition error:', error)
+     98:       setState(prev => ({ 
+     99:         ...prev, 
+    100:         isListening: false, 
+    101:         isProcessing: false,
+    102:         error: 'Voice recognition failed' 
+    103:       }))
+    104:       onError?.('Voice recognition failed')
+    105:     }
+    106:   }, [state.isListening, initializeAudio, onResult, onError])
+    107: 
+    108:   // Stop voice recognition
+    109:   const stopListening = useCallback(() => {
+    110:     if (timeoutRef.current) {
+    111:       clearTimeout(timeoutRef.current)
+    112:       timeoutRef.current = null
+    113:     }
+    114:     
+    115:     setState(prev => ({ 
+    116:       ...prev, 
+    117:       isListening: false, 
+    118:       isProcessing: false 
+    119:     }))
+    120:   }, [])
+    121: 
+    122:   // Speak text with automotive optimization
+    123:   const speak = useCallback(async (text: string) => {
+    124:     if (state.isSpeaking) {
+    125:       Speech.stop()
+    126:     }
+    127: 
+    128:     setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isSpeaking: true, error: null }))
+    129: 
+    130:     try {
+    131:       const speechOptions: Speech.SpeechOptions = {
+    132:         // Automotive optimizations
+    133:         rate: automotiveMode ? 0.85 : 1.0, // Slower for car environments
+    134:         pitch: 1.0,
+    135:         volume: automotiveMode ? 0.9 : 0.8, // Louder for road noise
+    136:         language: 'en-US',
+    137:         quality: Speech.VoiceQuality.Enhanced,
+    138:         onStart: () => {
+    139:           setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isSpeaking: true }))
+    140:         },
+    141:         onDone: () => {
+    142:           setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isSpeaking: false }))
+    143:         },
+    144:         onStopped: () => {
+    145:           setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isSpeaking: false }))
+    146:         },
+    147:         onError: (error) => {
+    148:           console.error('Speech synthesis error:', error)
+    149:           setState(prev => ({ 
+    150:             ...prev, 
+    151:             isSpeaking: false, 
+    152:             error: 'Speech synthesis failed' 
+    153:           }))
+    154:           onError?.('Speech synthesis failed')
+    155:         }
+    156:       }
+    157: 
+    158:       await Speech.speak(text, speechOptions)
+    159:       
+    160:     } catch (error) {
+    161:       console.error('Speech error:', error)
+    162:       setState(prev => ({ 
+    163:         ...prev, 
+    164:         isSpeaking: false, 
+    165:         error: 'Speech failed' 
+    166:       }))
+    167:       onError?.('Speech failed')
+    168:     }
+    169:   }, [state.isSpeaking, automotiveMode, onError])
+    170: 
+    171:   // Stop speaking
+    172:   const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {
+    173:     Speech.stop()
+    174:     setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isSpeaking: false }))
+    175:   }, [])
+    176: 
+    177:   // Get available voices (for settings)
+    178:   const getAvailableVoices = useCallback(async () => {
+    179:     try {
+    180:       const voices = await Speech.getAvailableVoicesAsync()
+    181:       return voices.filter(voice => voice.language.startsWith('en'))
+    182:     } catch (error) {
+    183:       console.error('Error getting voices:', error)
+    184:       return []
+    185:     }
+    186:   }, [])
+    187: 
+    188:   return {
+    189:     ...state,
+    190:     startListening,
+    191:     stopListening,

> ### Step 3.3: Create Enhanced Voice Button Component


üõ†Ô∏è  Using tool: fs_write (trusted)
 ‚ãÆ 
 ‚óè Path: /Users/saidachanda/development/dixon-smart-repair/product/wireframes/prototype/dixon-smart-repair-expo/components/voice-button.tsx

+      1: import React from 'react'
+      2: import {
+      3:   TouchableOpacity,
+      4:   Text,
+      5:   View,
+      6:   StyleSheet,
+      7:   Animated,
+      8: } from 'react-native'
+      9: import { useVoice } from '../hooks/use-voice'
+     10: 
+     11: interface VoiceButtonProps {
+     12:   onVoiceResult: (transcript: string) => void
+     13:   disabled?: boolean
+     14:   size?: 'small' | 'medium' | 'large'
+     15: }
+     16: 
+     17: export function VoiceButton({ onVoiceResult, disabled = false, size = 'medium' }: VoiceButtonProps) {
+     18:   const pulseAnim = React.useRef(new Animated.Value(1)).current
+     19:   
+     20:   const { 
+     21:     isListening, 
+     22:     isProcessing, 
+     23:     isSpeaking,
+     24:     startListening, 
+     25:     stopListening,
+     26:     error 
+     27:   } = useVoice({
+     28:     onResult: onVoiceResult,
+     29:     onError: (error) => {
+     30:       console.error('Voice error:', error)
+     31:     },
+     32:     automotiveMode: true
+     33:   })
+     34: 
+     35:   // Animate button when listening
+     36:   React.useEffect(() => {
+     37:     if (isListening) {
+     38:       const pulse = Animated.loop(
+     39:         Animated.sequence([
+     40:           Animated.timing(pulseAnim, {
+     41:             toValue: 1.2,
+     42:             duration: 800,
+     43:             useNativeDriver: true,
+     44:           }),
+     45:           Animated.timing(pulseAnim, {
+     46:             toValue: 1,
+     47:             duration: 800,
+     48:             useNativeDriver: true,
+     49:           }),
+     50:         ])
+     51:       )
+     52:       pulse.start()
+     53:       return () => pulse.stop()
+     54:     } else {
+     55:       pulseAnim.setValue(1)
+     56:     }
+     57:   }, [isListening, pulseAnim])
+     58: 
+     59:   const handlePress = () => {
+     60:     if (disabled) return
+     61:     
+     62:     if (isListening) {
+     63:       stopListening()
+     64:     } else {
+     65:       startListening()
+     66:     }
+     67:   }
+     68: 
+     69:   const getButtonStyle = () => {
+     70:     const baseStyle = [styles.voiceButton]
+     71:     
+     72:     if (size === 'small') baseStyle.push(styles.small)
+     73:     if (size === 'large') baseStyle.push(styles.large)
+     74:     
+     75:     if (isListening) {
+     76:       baseStyle.push(styles.listening)
+     77:     } else if (isProcessing) {
+     78:       baseStyle.push(styles.processing)
+     79:     } else if (disabled) {
+     80:       baseStyle.push(styles.disabled)
+     81:     }
+     82:     
+     83:     return baseStyle
+     84:   }
+     85: 
+     86:   const getIcon = () => {
+     87:     if (isProcessing) return '‚è≥'
+     88:     if (isListening) return 'üî¥'
+     89:     return 'üé§'
+     90:   }
+     91: 
+     92:   const getStatusText = () => {
+     93:     if (isProcessing) return 'Processing...'
+     94:     if (isListening) return 'Listening...'
+     95:     if (error) return 'Error'
+     96:     return null
+     97:   }
+     98: 
+     99:   return (
+    100:     <View style={styles.container}>
+    101:       <Animated.View style={{ transform: [{ scale: pulseAnim }] }}>
+    102:         <TouchableOpacity
+    103:           style={getButtonStyle()}
+    104:           onPress={handlePress}
+    105:           disabled={disabled || isProcessing}
+    106:           activeOpacity={0.7}
+    107:         >
+    108:           <Text style={styles.icon}>{getIcon()}</Text>
+    109:         </TouchableOpacity>
+    110:       </Animated.View>
+    111:       
+    112:       {getStatusText() && (
+    113:         <Text style={styles.statusText}>{getStatusText()}</Text>

> ### Step 3.4: Create Hands-Free Mode Component


üõ†Ô∏è  Using tool: fs_write (trusted)
 ‚ãÆ 
 ‚óè Path: /Users/saidachanda/development/dixon-smart-repair/product/wireframes/prototype/dixon-smart-repair-expo/components/hands-free-toggle.tsx

+      1: import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
+      2: import {
+      3:   View,
+      4:   Text,
+      5:   TouchableOpacity,
+      6:   StyleSheet,
+      7:   Animated,
+      8: } from 'react-native'
+      9: import { useVoice } from '../hooks/use-voice'
+     10: 
+     11: interface HandsFreeToggleProps {
+     12:   onVoiceResult: (transcript: string) => void
+     13:   enabled: boolean
+     14:   onToggle: (enabled: boolean) => void
+     15: }
+     16: 
+     17: export function HandsFreeToggle({ onVoiceResult, enabled, onToggle }: HandsFreeToggleProps) {
+     18:   const [isActive, setIsActive] = useState(false)
+     19:   const pulseAnim = React.useRef(new Animated.Value(1)).current
+     20:   
+     21:   const { 
+     22:     isListening, 
+     23:     isProcessing,
+     24:     startListening, 
+     25:     stopListening,
+     26:     speak,
+     27:     error 
+     28:   } = useVoice({
+     29:     onResult: (transcript) => {
+     30:       onVoiceResult(transcript)
+     31:       // In hands-free mode, automatically restart listening after processing
+     32:       if (enabled && !isProcessing) {
+     33:         setTimeout(() => {
+     34:           startListening()
+     35:         }, 2000) // Wait 2 seconds before listening again
+     36:       }
+     37:     },
+     38:     onError: (error) => {
+     39:       console.error('Hands-free voice error:', error)
+     40:       setIsActive(false)
+     41:     },
+     42:     automotiveMode: true
+     43:   })
+     44: 
+     45:   // Animate when active
+     46:   useEffect(() => {
+     47:     if (isActive && enabled) {
+     48:       const pulse = Animated.loop(
+     49:         Animated.sequence([
+     50:           Animated.timing(pulseAnim, {
+     51:             toValue: 1.1,
+     52:             duration: 1000,
+     53:             useNativeDriver: true,
+     54:           }),
+     55:           Animated.timing(pulseAnim, {
+     56:             toValue: 1,
+     57:             duration: 1000,
+     58:             useNativeDriver: true,
+     59:           }),
+     60:         ])
+     61:       )
+     62:       pulse.start()
+     63:       return () => pulse.stop()
+     64:     } else {
+     65:       pulseAnim.setValue(1)
+     66:     }
+     67:   }, [isActive, enabled, pulseAnim])
+     68: 
+     69:   // Handle hands-free mode toggle
+     70:   const handleToggle = async () => {
+     71:     const newEnabled = !enabled
+     72:     onToggle(newEnabled)
+     73:     
+     74:     if (newEnabled) {
+     75:       setIsActive(true)
+     76:       await speak("Hands-free mode activated. I'm listening for your vehicle issues.")
+     77:       setTimeout(() => {
+     78:         startListening()
+     79:       }, 1000)
+     80:     } else {
+     81:       setIsActive(false)
+     82:       stopListening()
+     83:       await speak("Hands-free mode deactivated.")
+     84:     }
+     85:   }
+     86: 
+     87:   const getStatusText = () => {
+     88:     if (!enabled) return 'Hands-Free: Off'
+     89:     if (isProcessing) return 'Processing...'
+     90:     if (isListening) return 'Listening...'
+     91:     if (isActive) return 'Hands-Free: Ready'
+     92:     return 'Hands-Free: On'
+     93:   }
+     94: 
+     95:   const getStatusColor = () => {
+     96:     if (!enabled) return '#64748b'
+     97:     if (isListening) return '#ef4444'
+     98:     if (isProcessing) return '#f59e0b'
+     99:     return '#16a34a'
+    100:   }
+    101: 
+    102:   return (
+    103:     <View style={styles.container}>
+    104:       <Animated.View style={{ transform: [{ scale: pulseAnim }] }}>
+    105:         <TouchableOpacity
+    106:           style={[
+    107:             styles.toggleButton,
+    108:             enabled && styles.toggleButtonActive,
+    109:             isListening && styles.toggleButtonListening,
+    110:           ]}
+    111:           onPress={handleToggle}
+    112:           activeOpacity={0.7}
+    113:         >
+    114:           <View style={styles.toggleContent}>
+    115:             <Text style={styles.toggleIcon}>
+    116:               {enabled ? (isListening ? 'üî¥' : 'üéôÔ∏è') : 'üîá'}
+    117:             </Text>
+    118:             <Text style={[
+    119:               styles.toggleText,
+    120:               enabled && styles.toggleTextActive
+    121:             ]}>
+    122:               Hands-Free
+    123:             </Text>
+    124:           </View>
+    125:         </TouchableOpacity>
+    126:       </Animated.View>
+    127:       
+    128:       <Text style={[styles.statusText, { color: getStatusColor() }]}>
+    129:         {getStatusText()}
+    130:       </Text>
+    131:       
+    132:       {error && (
+    133:         <Text style={styles.errorText}>
+    134:           Voice error - hands-free disabled
+    135:         </Text>
+    136:       )}
+    137:       
+    138:       {enabled && (
+    139:         <Text style={styles.helpText}>
+    140:           Speak naturally about your vehicle issues
+    141:         </Text>
+    142:       )}
+    143:     </View>
+    144:   )
+    145: }
+    146: 
+    147: const styles = StyleSheet.create({
+    148:   container: {
+    149:     alignItems: 'center',
+    150:     padding: 16,
+    151:   },
+    152:   toggleButton: {
+    153:     backgroundColor: '#f1f5f9',
+    154:     paddingHorizontal: 20,
+    155:     paddingVertical: 12,
+    156:     borderRadius: 24,
+    157:     borderWidth: 2,
+    158:     borderColor: '#e2e8f0',
+    159:     minWidth: 120,
+    160:     elevation: 2,
+    161:     shadowColor: '#000',
+    162:     shadowOffset: { width: 0, height: 2 },
+    163:     shadowOpacity: 0.1,
+    164:     shadowRadius: 4,
+    165:   },
+    166:   toggleButtonActive: {
+    167:     backgroundColor: '#dcfce7',
+    168:     borderColor: '#16a34a',
+    169:   },
+    170:   toggleButtonListening: {
+    171:     backgroundColor: '#fecaca',
+    172:     borderColor: '#ef4444',
+    173:   },
+    174:   toggleContent: {
+    175:     flexDirection: 'row',
+    176:     alignItems: 'center',
+    177:     justifyContent: 'center',
+    178:   },
+    179:   toggleIcon: {
+    180:     fontSize: 16,
+    181:     marginRight: 8,
+    182:   },
+    183:   toggleText: {
+    184:     fontSize: 14,
+    185:     fontWeight: '600',
+    186:     color: '#64748b',
+    187:   },
+    188:   toggleTextActive: {
+    189:     color: '#16a34a',
+    190:   },
+    191:   statusText: {
+    192:     fontSize: 12,
+    193:     fontWeight: '500',
+    194:     marginTop: 8,
+    195:   },
+    196:   errorText: {
+    197:     fontSize: 12,
+    198:     color: '#ef4444',
+    199:     marginTop: 4,
+    200:     textAlign: 'center',
+    201:   },
+    202:   helpText: {
+    203:     fontSize: 11,
+    204:     color: '#64748b',

+    206:     textAlign: 'center',
+    207:     fontStyle: 'italic',
+    208:   },
+    209: })

> ### Step 3.5: Create Camera Integration for VIN Scanning


üõ†Ô∏è  Using tool: fs_write (trusted)
 ‚ãÆ 
 ‚óè Path: /Users/saidachanda/development/dixon-smart-repair/product/wireframes/prototype/dixon-smart-repair-expo/components/camera-scanner.tsx

+      1: import React, { useState, useRef } from 'react'
+      2: import {
+      3:   View,
+      4:   Text,
+      5:   TouchableOpacity,
+      6:   StyleSheet,
+      7:   Modal,
+      8:   Alert,
+      9:   Dimensions,
+     10: } from 'react-native'
+     11: import { CameraView, CameraType, useCameraPermissions } from 'expo-camera'
+     12: import * as ImagePicker from 'expo-image-picker'
+     13: 
+     14: interface CameraScannerProps {
+     15:   visible: boolean
+     16:   onClose: () => void
+     17:   onVinDetected: (vin: string) => void
+     18:   onPhotoTaken: (uri: string) => void
+     19: }
+     20: 
+     21: const { width, height } = Dimensions.get('window')
+     22: 
+     23: export function CameraScanner({ visible, onClose, onVinDetected, onPhotoTaken }: CameraScannerProps) {
+     24:   const [facing, setFacing] = useState<CameraType>('back')
+     25:   const [permission, requestPermission] = useCameraPermissions()
+     26:   const [isScanning, setIsScanning] = useState(false)
+     27:   const cameraRef = useRef<CameraView>(null)
+     28: 
+     29:   // Mock VIN patterns for demonstration
+     30:   const mockVins = [
+     31:     '1HGBH41JXMN109186', // Honda
+     32:     '4T1C11AK8LU123456', // Toyota
+     33:     '1FTFW1ET5DFC10312', // Ford
+     34:     '1G1ZT53806F109149', // Chevrolet
+     35:     'WBAVA33598NL12345', // BMW
+     36:   ]
+     37: 
+     38:   const handlePermissionRequest = async () => {
+     39:     if (!permission?.granted) {
+     40:       const result = await requestPermission()
+     41:       return result.granted
+     42:     }
+     43:     return true
+     44:   }
+     45: 
+     46:   const handleTakePhoto = async () => {
+     47:     if (!cameraRef.current) return
+     48: 
+     49:     try {
+     50:       setIsScanning(true)
+     51:       const photo = await cameraRef.current.takePictureAsync({
+     52:         quality: 0.8,
+     53:         base64: false,
+     54:       })
+     55: 
+     56:       if (photo?.uri) {
+     57:         onPhotoTaken(photo.uri)
+     58:         
+     59:         // Simulate VIN detection from photo
+     60:         setTimeout(() => {
+     61:           const randomVin = mockVins[Math.floor(Math.random() * mockVins.length)]
+     62:           onVinDetected(randomVin)
+     63:           setIsScanning(false)
+     64:           onClose()
+     65:         }, 2000)
+     66:       }
+     67:     } catch (error) {
+     68:       console.error('Camera error:', error)
+     69:       Alert.alert('Camera Error', 'Failed to take photo')
+     70:       setIsScanning(false)
+     71:     }
+     72:   }
+     73: 
+     74:   const handlePickImage = async () => {
+     75:     try {
+     76:       const result = await ImagePicker.launchImageLibraryAsync({
+     77:         mediaTypes: ImagePicker.MediaTypeOptions.Images,
+     78:         allowsEditing: true,
+     79:         aspect: [16, 9],
+     80:         quality: 0.8,
+     81:       })
+     82: 
+     83:       if (!result.canceled && result.assets[0]) {
+     84:         const uri = result.assets[0].uri
+     85:         onPhotoTaken(uri)
+     86:         
+     87:         // Simulate VIN detection from uploaded image
+     88:         setTimeout(() => {
+     89:           const randomVin = mockVins[Math.floor(Math.random() * mockVins.length)]
+     90:           onVinDetected(randomVin)
+     91:           onClose()
+     92:         }, 1500)
+     93:       }
+     94:     } catch (error) {
+     95:       console.error('Image picker error:', error)
+     96:       Alert.alert('Error', 'Failed to pick image')
+     97:     }
+     98:   }
+     99: 
+    100:   const toggleCameraFacing = () => {
+    101:     setFacing(current => (current === 'back' ? 'front' : 'back'))
+    102:   }
+    103: 
+    104:   if (!permission) {
+    105:     return <View />
+    106:   }
+    107: 
+    108:   if (!permission.granted) {
+    109:     return (
+    110:       <Modal visible={visible} animationType="slide">
+    111:         <View style={styles.permissionContainer}>
+    112:           <Text style={styles.permissionTitle}>Camera Permission Required</Text>
+    113:           <Text style={styles.permissionText}>
+    114:             Dixon Smart Repair needs camera access to scan VIN numbers and capture vehicle issues.
+    115:           </Text>
+    116:           <TouchableOpacity style={styles.permissionButton} onPress={handlePermissionRequest}>
+    117:             <Text style={styles.permissionButtonText}>Grant Permission</Text>
+    118:           </TouchableOpacity>
+    119:           <TouchableOpacity style={styles.cancelButton} onPress={onClose}>
+    120:             <Text style={styles.cancelButtonText}>Cancel</Text>
+    121:           </TouchableOpacity>
+    122:         </View>
+    123:       </Modal>
+    124:     )
+    125:   }
+    126: 
+    127:   return (
+    128:     <Modal visible={visible} animationType="slide">
+    129:       <View style={styles.container}>
+    130:         <CameraView
+    131:           ref={cameraRef}
+    132:           style={styles.camera}
+    133:           facing={facing}
+    134:         >
+    135:           {/* Header */}
+    136:           <View style={styles.header}>
+    137:             <TouchableOpacity style={styles.closeButton} onPress={onClose}>
+    138:               <Text style={styles.closeButtonText}>√ó</Text>
+    139:             </TouchableOpacity>
+    140:             <Text style={styles.headerTitle}>Scan VIN or Take Photo</Text>
+    141:             <TouchableOpacity style={styles.flipButton} onPress={toggleCameraFacing}>
+    142:               <Text style={styles.flipButtonText}>üîÑ</Text>
+    143:             </TouchableOpacity>
+    144:           </View>
+    145: 
+    146:           {/* VIN Scanning Overlay */}
+    147:           <View style={styles.overlay}>
+    148:             <View style={styles.scanArea}>
+    149:               <View style={styles.scanFrame} />
+    150:               <Text style={styles.scanText}>
+    151:                 {isScanning ? 'Scanning VIN...' : 'Position VIN within frame'}
+    152:               </Text>
+    153:             </View>
+    154:           </View>
+    155: 
+    156:           {/* Controls */}
+    157:           <View style={styles.controls}>
+    158:             <TouchableOpacity style={styles.galleryButton} onPress={handlePickImage}>
+    159:               <Text style={styles.controlButtonText}>üì∑</Text>
+    160:               <Text style={styles.controlLabel}>Gallery</Text>
+    161:             </TouchableOpacity>
+    162: 
+    163:             <TouchableOpacity 
+    164:               style={[styles.captureButton, isScanning && styles.captureButtonScanning]} 
+    165:               onPress={handleTakePhoto}
+    166:               disabled={isScanning}
+    167:             >
+    168:               <View style={styles.captureButtonInner} />
+    169:             </TouchableOpacity>
+    170: 
+    171:             <TouchableOpacity style={styles.manualButton} onPress={() => {
+    172:               onClose()
+    173:               // Could trigger manual VIN entry
+    174:             }}>
+    175:               <Text style={styles.controlButtonText}>‚å®Ô∏è</Text>
+    176:               <Text style={styles.controlLabel}>Manual</Text>
+    177:             </TouchableOpacity>
+    178:           </View>
+    179:         </CameraView>
+    180:       </View>
+    181:     </Modal>
+    182:   )
+    183: }
+    184: 
+    185: const styles = StyleSheet.create({
+    186:   container: {
+    187:     flex: 1,
+    188:     backgroundColor: '#000',
+    189:   },

+    192:   },
